<s> CHAPTER XIX High up in one of the topmost chambers of the Hotel Plaza, Nikasti, after his conference with Von Schwerin and Fischer, sought solitude </s>
<s> He opened the high windows, out of which he could scarcely see, dragged up a chest of drawers and perched himself, Oriental fashion, on the top, his long yellow fingers intertwined around his knees, his soft brown eyes gazing over the wooded slopes of the Park </s>
<s> He was away from the clamour of tongues, from the poisoned clouds of sophistry, even from the disturbance of his own thoughts, incited by specious arguments to some form of reciprocity </s>
<s> Here he sat in the clouds and searched for the true things </s>
<s> His eyes seemed to be travelling over the battlefields of Europe </s>
<s> He saw the swaying fortunes of mighty armies, he looked into council chambers, he seemed to feel the pulses of the great world force which kept going this most amazing Juggernaut </s>
<s> He saw the furnaces of Japan, blazing by night and day; saw the forms of hundreds of thousands of his fellow creatures bent to their task; saw the streams of ships leaving his ports, laden down with stores; saw the great guns speeding across Siberia, the endless trains of ammunition, the rifles, food for the famine-stricken giants who beat upon the air with empty fists </s>
<s> He saw the gold come streaming back </s>
<s> He saw it poured into the banks, the pockets of the merchants, the homes of his people </s>
<s> He saw brightening days throughout the land </s>
<s> He saw the slow but splendid strength of the nation rejoicing in its new possibilities </s>
<s> And beyond that, what </s>
<s> Wealth was the great means towards the great end, but if the great end were once lost sight of, there was no more hideous poison than that stream of enervating prosperity </s>
<s> He remembered his own diatribes concerning the decadence of England; how he had pointed to the gold poison, to the easy living of the poor, the blatant luxury of the rich </s>
<s> He had pointed to the soft limbs, the cities which had become pools of sensuality, to the daily life which, calling for no effort, had seen the passing of the spirit and the triumph of the gross </s>
<s> And what about his own people </s>
<s> Mankind was the same the world over </s>
<s> The gold which was bringing strength and life to the nation might very soon exude the same poisonous fumes, might very soon be laying its thrall upon a people to whom living had become an easier thing </s>
<s> However it might be for other, the Western nations, for his own he firmly believed that war alone, with its thousand privations, its call to the chivalry of his people, was the one great safeguard </s>
<s> China </s>
<s> The days had gone by when the taking of China could inspire </s>
<s> It was to greater things they must look </s>
<s> Australia </s>
<s> New Zealand </s>
<s> Had any Western race the right to flaunt her Empire's flag in Asiatic seas </s>
<s> And America </s>
<s> Once again he felt the slow rising of wrath as he recalled the insults of past years .. </s>
<s> the adventurous sons of his country treated like savages and negroes by that uncultured, strong-limbed race of coarse-fibered, unimaginative materialists </s>
<s> There was a call, indeed, to the soul of his country to avenge, to make safe, the homes and lives of her colonists </s>
<s> Across the seas he looked into the council chambers of the wise men of his race </s>
<s> He saw the men whose word would tell </s>
<s> He watched their faces turned towards him, waiting; heard the beginning of the conflict of thoughts and minds--blind fidelity to the cause which they had espoused, or a rougher, more splendid, more selfish stroke for the greatness of Japan and Japan only </s>
<s> "If we break our faith we lose our honour," one murmured </s>
<s> "There is no honour save the care of my people," he heard one of his greatest countrymen reply </s>
<s> So he sat and thought, revolved in his mind arguments, morals, philosophy </s>
<s> It was the problem which had confronted the great Emperor, his own ancestor, who had lived for three months on the floor of the Temple, asking but one question of the Silent Powers: "Through what gate shall I lead my nation to greatness" </s>
<s> The senses of the man who crouched in his curious attitude, with his eyes still piercing the heavens, were mobile and extraordinary things </s>
<s> No disturbing sounds had reached him from outside </s>
<s> His isolation seemed complete and impregnable </s>
<s> Yet, without turning his head, he was perfectly conscious of the slow opening of the door </s>
<s> His whole frame stiffened </s>
<s> He was conscious for one bitter second of a lapse from the careful guarding of his ways </s>
<s> That second passed, however, and left him prepared even for danger, his brain and muscles alike tense </s>
<s> He turned his head </s>
<s> The expression of slow surprise, which even parted his lips and narrowed his eyes, was only half assumed </s>
<s> "What do you wish" </s>
<s> he asked </s>
<s> Lutchester did not for a moment reply </s>

<s> He slipped down to the ground </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXII Mrs Theodore Hastings was forty-eight years old, which her friends said was the reason why her mansion on Fifth Avenue was furnished and lit with the delicate sombreness of an old Italian palace </s>
<s> There was about it none of the garishness, the almost resplendent brilliancy associated with the abodes of many of our neighbours </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXVI Lutchester left Sonia and the Ritz-Carlton a few minutes before midnight, to find a great yellow moon overhead, which seemed to have risen somewhere at the back of Central Park </s>
<s> The broad thoroughfare up which he turned seemed to have developed a new and unfamiliar beauty </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXVII Fischer, as he waited for Pamela the following afternoon in the sitting-room of her flat on Fifty-eighth Street, felt that although the practical future of his life might be decided in other places, it was here that its real climax would be reached </s>
<s> Pamela herself was to pronounce sentence upon him </s>
<s> He was feeling scarcely at his best </s>
<s> An examination in the courthouse, which he had imagined would last only a few minutes, had been protracted throughout the afternoon </s>
<s> The district attorney had asked him a great many questions, some rather awkward ones, and the inquiry itself had been almost grudgingly adjourned for a few hours </s>

<s> Fischer pushed the newspaper impatiently away, and, in the act of doing so, the door was opened and Pamela entered </s>

<s> "I see you are looking at the account of your misdeeds," she said, as she seated herself behind a tea tray </s>

<s> Fischer frowned irritably </s>
<s> "For four hours," he complained, "several lawyers and a most inquisitive police captain have been asking me the same question in a hundred different ways </s>

<s> I was only trusting him for a matter of a few hours" </s>

<s> "What have you come to discuss, Mr Fischer" </s>

<s> "If you give me any encouragement, I can put before you a great proposition </s>

<s> What have I to do with any proposition you may have to make" </s>
<s> "Just this," he explained </s>
<s> "I have a serious and authentic proposition to make to the American Government </s>
<s> I cannot make it officially-- although it comes from the highest of all sources--for the most obvious reasons </s>

<s> That is because you believed in British invincibility upon the sea </s>
<s> I never did" </s>
<s> "Go on, please," Pamela begged </s>
<s> "I am still waiting to realise my position in all this" </s>
<s> "I should like," Fischer declared, "my proposition to reach the President through Senator Hastings, and Senator Hastings is your uncle" </s>
<s> "I see," Pamela murmured </s>
<s> "My offer itself is a very simple one," Fischer continued </s>
<s> "Your secret service is so bad that you probably know nothing of what is happening </s>
<s> Ours, on the other hand, is still marvellously good, and what I am going to tell you is surely the truth </s>
<s> Japan is accumulating great wealth </s>
<s> She is saving her ships and men for one purpose, and one purpose only </s>
<s> Europe could not bribe her highly enough to take a more active part in this war </s>
<s> Her price was one which could not be paid </s>
<s> She demanded a free hand with the United States" </s>
<s> "This," Pamela admitted, "is quite interesting, but it is entirely in the realms of conjecture, is it not" </s>
<s> "Not wholly," Fischer insisted </s>
<s> "At the proper time I should be prepared to bring you evidence that tentative proposals were made by Japan to both England and France, asking what would be their attitude, should she provide them with half a million men and undertake transport, if at the conclusion of the war she desired a settlement with the United States </s>
<s> The answer from France and England was the same--that they could not countenance an inimical attitude towards the States" </s>

<s> "England would sell her soul, but not for a mess of pottage </s>
<s> To proceed, however, Japan has practically kept out of the war </s>
<s> She is enjoying a prosperity never known before, and for every million pounds' worth of munitions she exports to Russia, she puts calmly on one side twenty-five per cent, to accumulate for her own use </s>

<s> CHAPTER XXXII Lutchester breathed the air of Washington and felt almost homesick </s>
<s> The stateliness of the city, its sedate and quiescent air after the turmoil of New York, impressed him profoundly </s>
<s> Everywhere its diplomatic associations made themselves felt </s>

<s> Lutchester repeated </s>
<s> His host smiled as he led the way to the piazza steps </s>
<s> Pamela had already stepped into the boat, and with the help of a boatman was adjusting the sail </s>
<s> She waved her hand gaily and pointed to the level stretch of placid water, still faintly brilliant in the dying sunlight </s>
<s> "You think that we shall reach Misery Island before the tide turns" </s>
<s> she called out </s>
<s> Lutchester stepped lightly into the boat and took the place to which she pointed </s>
<s> "I am content," he said, "to take my chance" </s>
<s> THE END </s>
